Hefei Organizes Drought Relief Committee 108

This county is experiencing a drought unprecedented in decades, with yellow dust and white grass, scarcely any green to be seen. Ponds and pools are completely dry, and no late rice can be harvested. Rice prices have already risen from two dou per yuan to less than one dou, while hoarders continue to speculate and transport grain out of the area. The suffering of the common people is unbearable to witness. Various public organizations, deeply saddened by the situation, held a meeting at the county government office at noon on the 7th to discuss relief measures. They decided to establish a Drought Relief Committee, comprising representatives from various public organizations, schools, and district chiefs as ex officio members. Thirty-six people, including Fei Yongzhang, Yang Licuo, and Kong Huaqing, were elected as committee members. Furthermore, eleven individuals from the county government, the Party headquarters, and the Red Swastika Society were mutually elected as standing committee members. Subsequently, Battalion Commander Ruan Zijing, stationed in Yun, proposed a ban on rice and grain transportation out of the river area starting from the 8th, which was unanimously approved. It was also agreed that the inaugural meeting of the Drought Relief Committee would be held at the Red Swastika Society on the 8th.

Page 11

Municipal News, Social Affairs Bureau

Holding Registration of Imported Foreign Rice 109

Rice Shortage Estimated at Around Ten Million Piculs, Panic Expected by Next Spring

Soaring Rice Prices Are the Result of Rice Merchants' Speculation

Tax-Exempt Import of Foreign Rice Difficult to Implement Immediately

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, this summer, various parts of the world have suffered from floods and droughts, resulting in poor harvests. Both northern and southern provinces of China have also encountered difficulties, and grain shortages are inevitable. Consequently, merchants and influential figures in the money lending industry in this city have been eagerly ordering foreign rice to profit from the situation. The Municipal Grain Management Committee has even approved a resolution to allow merchants to order forward foreign rice imports under bond to alleviate the domestic grain panic. Yesterday, a reporter from Shen Shi News Agency visited Mr. Wu Huanru, the head of the Second Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, who provided detailed information on the subsequent relief efforts for the rice shortage and the planned measures to regulate the situation as follows:

Holding Registration of Imported Foreign Rice 110

According to Mr. Wu, the severe drought this summer has led to poor harvests in various regions, causing a shortage of rice. It is inevitable to rely on foreign rice imports for relief. However, the import of foreign rice should aim to meet the needs of the inland areas and should not be unrestricted. Now merchants are ordering foreign rice as a source of profit, placing large-scale advance orders. Even the money lending industry is investing huge amounts of capital in the grain business, waiting for favorable prices to sell. If the quantities ordered are indeed needed by consumers, there is no problem. Otherwise, if the goods cannot be sold in the future and rice prices fall, the losses may be small, but the outflow of money will affect the national economy, which would be unimaginable. Therefore, the Social Affairs Bureau has now decided to instruct the Grains and Cereals Trade Association that all merchants ordering foreign rice must first register with the Social Affairs Bureau for statistical purposes. Once imports reach a certain limit, efforts can be made to stop operations to prevent merchants from losing money.

Harvest Shortfall Not as Severe as Anticipated 111

The rice-producing provinces in Jiangnan have all suffered from unprecedented droughts. Rice merchants are hoarding rice, hoping to profit from the speculation. The rice price has already risen to above the 13-yuan limit price, and the future remains uncertain. However, the harvest shortfall in various provinces is not as severe as anticipated. The most severely affected area is Zhejiang Province, with an estimated harvest of only about 30% of a normal year. However, Zhejiang's grain supply has always been insufficient, and the drought will undoubtedly exacerbate the situation. The estimated grain shortage for the year is below ten million piculs. In Jiangsu, there are still areas with good harvests in the Jiangbei region, while the Jiangnan region has a limited shortage, with a maximum shortage of about two to three million piculs. Southern Anhui can still be self-sufficient, while the disaster in northern Anhui is more severe. According to statistics from the Jiangxi Grain Administration, the province has a shortage of about one million piculs. Hunan and Hubei are generally offsetting each other. If the autumn grains, such as buckwheat, taro, corn, millet, sorghum, can have good harvests, and if wheat can be planted effectively next spring with favorable weather conditions, the rice shortage can be compensated for. Moreover, relatively well-off families in rural areas often hoard rice for many years to prepare for famine. Based on the above observations, although there is a rice shortage, it is only around ten million piculs, which does not necessarily require foreign rice for relief. However, it is definitely not as severe as anticipated, and the panic period should be during the transition between the old and new crops next year. The situation can be maintained in a normal state within the year. The recent soaring rice prices are not due to supply exceeding demand, but rather the result of rice merchants' speculation. Once strict restrictions are imposed, it will not be difficult to suppress them. It is expected that there may be a significant reaction and decline in the prices in October or November this winter, which is something that all hoarders should pay attention to.

Forward Foreign Rice Imports under Bond 112

Mr. Wu continued, the grain panic next spring is inevitable. I previously drafted a plan to allow rice merchants to order forward foreign rice under bond and submitted it to the Grain Management Committee for resolution, together with the Zhejiang Provincial Government, to request approval from the Executive Yuan. The plan stipulates that the selling price should not exceed 12 yuan. If the rice price falls below 9 yuan at that time, the import tax on foreign rice will be fully exempted. If the rice price is at 9 yuan, the import tax on foreign rice will be reduced by half. If the rice price is above 10 yuan, the import tax on foreign rice will be fully levied. This measure is effective in regulating the grain supply and suppressing prices. However, due to its complexity, it has not been understood and agreed upon by the relevant parties, and it may not be easily implemented at this time.

Foreign Rice Should Be Transported by National Vessels 113

Shipping Association Submits Petition to Social Affairs Bureau

Please Instruct Bean and Rice Merchants to Comply

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, due to the severe drought and poor harvests in various regions, bean and rice merchants are busily procuring foreign rice to regulate the people's food supply. As of now, the total amount has reached 300,000 piculs. The Shanghai Shipping Association points out that the areas where foreign rice is procured are Saigon in Annam, Rangoon in Burma, and Bangkok in Siam. The foreign rice procured by rice merchants is delivered locally and must be transported by ships. Therefore, the association has submitted a petition to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, requesting that the bean and rice merchants be instructed to use national vessels for all foreign rice procurement to recover the benefits.

Yang Dezhao Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 114

Will Visit Chiang in Lushan after Staying for a Day or Two

According to the Central News Agency, Yang Dezhao, the representative of Chen Jitang, the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army, who was stationed in Nanjing, returned to Guangdong last month to report on the situation in Nanjing. His mission has been completed. Yesterday afternoon, at 2:30 PM, he arrived in Shanghai aboard the Changxing Company's Asia Queen liner. His wife and others were there to greet him at the port. After disembarking, Mr. Yang returned to his private residence for rest. He is scheduled to visit Chairman Chiang in Lushan within the next few days. A Central News Agency reporter met Mr. Yang on the ship yesterday and asked him the following questions:

Chen Jitang Finds It Difficult to Go North for the Time Being 115

Mr. Yang denied the rumor that he was carrying a personal letter from Chairman Chiang to Chen Jitang this time. He stated that in addition to reporting his mission in Nanjing to Mr. Chen, he also returned to his hometown to inspect schools and mining organizations. This was purely a personal matter. As for the news that Chen Jitang would be coming to Nanjing and Shanghai for inspection, Mr. Chen himself had the intention, but due to the complexity of military and political affairs, he believed it would not be possible for the time being. Xiao Focheng has not returned to Siam since returning to China and has no intention of going there again.

Joint Bandit Suppression to Launch General Offensive Immediately 116

As for the joint suppression of the remnants of bandits in Fujian and Jiangxi by the southeastern routes, the deployment of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army has now been completed. As soon as the autumn weather cools down, a general offensive can be launched immediately. The central government's monthly subsidy for the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army has not yet been increased. Mr. Yang denied reports that he was ordered to go to Fujian to meet with Chen Yi, the Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, to discuss the joint bandit suppression by the southeastern routes, stating that he had not left Guangdong to go to Fujian.

Guangdong and Hong Kong Central Committee Members Have No Indication at Present 117

The members of the Central Committee in Guangdong and Hong Kong have not yet expressed their views on the convocation of the Fifth National Congress. However, at this time of national crisis, they share the same determination with the central government to unite and save the country. As for whether the issue of abolishing the two southwestern organs will be submitted to the Fifth National Congress for discussion, no decision has been made yet.

Will Go to Lushan After a Short Rest 118

Mr. Yang intends to stay in Shanghai for a day or two to rest after the arduous journey, and then go to Lushan to visit Chairman Chiang. His wife and others also plan to go with him. However, he stated that the reports that he would go to Jiangxi to participate in the Lushan conference were inaccurate.

Special Envoy of the New King of Belgium

Johnson Did Not Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 119

Expected to Arrive in Port by Ship on the 27th

Will Stay for One Night and Then Cross to the East the Next Day

Will Visit Chairman Lin in China Again Next Month

Following the royal tradition, the new King of Belgium has specially dispatched Baron Johnson as his special envoy to the countries of the Far East to pay his respects. It was reported yesterday that he was arriving in Shanghai from the South Sea Islands aboard the Java Company's Tjimindie liner. A reporter from this newspaper specifically visited the Belgian Consulate yesterday, and it was said that the consulate had received unofficial news that Special Envoy Johnson would arrive in Shanghai aboard the French mail ship Aramis on the 27th of this month, and would cross to the East on the original ship the next day. He will come to China again in mid-September to meet with the central authorities. The rumors were not confirmed.

Origin of the Mission 120

King Leopold III, the new King of Belgium, has demonstrated remarkable political achievements since he ascended the throne this spring. Following the royal tradition, he has specially dispatched a special envoy to visit various countries. The mission is to inform the heads of friendly nations of the death of the late King Albert, the new King's ascension to the throne, and to thank the friendly nations for their enthusiasm in participating in the above two ceremonies, thereby strengthening diplomatic ties.

Preparing for a Welcome 121

After being appointed, Special Envoy Johnson, along with his wife and staff, departed from Belgium on June 29 and first went to the South Sea Islands, stopping in Batavia, and then taking the French mail ship Aramis to China. The ship is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 27th of this month, and it is learned that the Belgian Consul General in Shanghai, Tan Erfu, has prepared for welcoming and entertaining him after receiving the news.

Visiting China 122

It is reported that Special Envoy Johnson will stay in Shanghai for one night after arriving in Shanghai, and will cross to the East by ship the next day. He is scheduled to come to China again on September 12, first to Tianjin and Beijing, and then to the capital to meet with Chairman Lin of the National Government to thank the National Government for its sincerity in offering condolences and congratulations. At the same time, he will visit Premier Wang and others, and plan to go to Jiangxi to visit Chairman Chiang, and take the opportunity to travel to famous scenic spots in the north and south of China, and investigate the construction of China. He will stay in China for about two weeks before returning to Belgium.

Johnson's Brief History 123

Baron Johnson, the special envoy dispatched to China this time, is currently the general manager of the Belgian Silver Company, is rich in assets, and is one of the leaders of the Belgian financial community. Considering that the King of Belgium has sent special envoys to China, this is the second time, the first time being in 1910, 35 years ago. After the first special envoy came to China, there was a great deal of progress in China-Belgium trade and investment, and in the friendship between China and Belgium.

Tan Xihong Dispatched by the Ministry of Industry

To Shanghai to Investigate Silk Factories 124

Silk Prices Plummet, Manufacturers Unable to Maintain Operations

Investigate the Current Situation to Seek Fundamental Relief

Due to the impact of Japanese silk dumping during the new cocoon season, silk prices in Shanghai have plummeted, resulting in excessive losses, making it impossible for manufacturers to maintain operations. However, for the sake of the livelihood of workers and social security, they are reluctant to let them suffer the pain of unemployment. It is estimated that only 33 factories in the city are barely operating, and five of them have been forced to shut down one after another, making the future of the silk industry increasingly bleak. In order to seek relief, the authorities of the Executive Yuan have instructed the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to formulate relief measures, and the two ministries have separately planned and decided on four model principles. The Ministry of Industry has dispatched Tan Xihong, the director of the Department of Agriculture, to Shanghai to investigate the current situation of production and sales of silk factories, and the truth about the losses, in order to seek fundamental relief. It is learned that Mr. Tan arrived in Shanghai by overnight express yesterday morning and will conduct separate investigations. He will return to Beijing in about a week to report on his mission.

Dispute over Strike of Yellow Automobile Workers

Resolved Yesterday Through Mediation 125

Social Affairs Bureau Sent Representatives to Supervise the Signing of Eight-Article Agreement

All Workers Scheduled to Resume Work at 7:00 AM on the 14th

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the drivers and workers of the Shanghai Chinese Yellow Automobile Company went on strike in the early morning of the previous day due to dissatisfaction with the company's unwarranted dismissal of workers and poor treatment, the Social Affairs Bureau sent representatives to mediate yesterday, and an eight-article agreement was signed, declaring a resolution. The workers are scheduled to resume work on the 14th.

Resolution Reached: The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau considered the strike by the company's workers to be a major event, so even though yesterday was a regular holiday, it still sent Wang Xianqing, the director of the Mediation Section of the Third Division, to the company on Pushi Road to mediate. Wang Xianqing served as chairman, and the representatives of the management, Lin Zhongming, the representatives of the drivers' union, Zhu Weichang, Chen Daofu, and Yu Damin, and the representatives of the workers, Cheng Rongsheng, Zhang Genfu, and Zhu Guoliang, first stated their experiences, and then the chairman summarized the opinions of both parties and made exhortations.

As a result of the signing of the agreement, both parties reached an agreement and signed the agreement until 9:00 PM. The original text is as follows: (1) All drivers are allowed to resume work uniformly at 7:00 AM on the 14th of this month, and wages will not be deducted. (2) The work system will be implemented in accordance with the new regulations promulgated by the company on August 1st of this year. Starting from September 1st, the rest shift will be increased by three workers. (3) The compensation for Chi Miaogen, Zhou Huicheng, Yan Asan, and others is allowed to be waived. (4) Ren Changshan is allowed to work as usual. (5) The amendment of the driver's service regulations and the improvement of treatment conditions will be waited for the party and government organs to handle in accordance with the law. (6) The company will pay 150 yuan of compensation for Zhou Yintai, which will be refunded 20 yuan, and the rest will be waived. (7) Wang Langen is required to pay 43 yuan for damage repair fees, which will be reduced by 20 yuan. (8) The union should be responsible for publishing a statement in the newspaper to clarify the misunderstanding caused by the sudden strike of the workers this time.

Article 9 of the Savings Bank Law

Banking Association Studies Implementation Regulations 130

Requests to Amend Various Articles Have Not Yet Been Replied to

Documents Submitted by Non-Member Banks to be Drafted Today

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the promulgation of the Savings Bank Law, the banking industry association requested amendments to Articles 5, 7, 8, and 15. A subcommittee has been formed for Article 9 and will meet today to study it. The details are as follows:

Request for Amendments 131

The banking industry association has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance to delete the restriction in Article 5 that the total amount of current deposits should not exceed 40%, to delete Articles 7.4 and 7.5, to delete the restrictions on the composition of Article 8, and to amend Article 15 and the restrictions on lending to rural areas in Article 8. As of yesterday, no reply has been received from the Yuan and the Ministry. After all non-members agree with the association's documents, they will be corrected today and sent to the non-member banks for sealing, so that they can be submitted to the Yuan and the Ministry for approval.

Studying Implementation 132

After the 53rd executive committee meeting of the banking industry association decided to form a subcommittee to study Article 9 of the Savings Bank Law, it has been decided to convene a subcommittee meeting this afternoon to study how to implement and manage it. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned from the banking industry yesterday that the banking association has never opposed Article 9 in principle. It initially requested a delay in implementation when requesting amendments to the entire Savings Law. After receiving the order from the Ministry of Finance, it has decided to form a subcommittee to study how to implement it.

Lin Kanghou Talks 133

A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency visited Lin Kanghou, the secretary-general of the banking association, yesterday and asked him about this matter. According to him, the association absolutely agrees with this matter in principle, but because the content of Article 9 of the law is very complicated, the guaranteed assets, types, numbers, and management should be explained in detail and clearly divided, otherwise it will be difficult to implement. Moreover, the Ministry's order that government bonds and treasury bills must be calculated according to market prices is also inappropriate, because government bonds and treasury bills are guaranteed by national tax revenue, and their prices should not be calculated according to market prices. I feel that there are many Chinese and foreign banks in Shanghai, and if the government strictly enforces this law on Chinese banks, it cannot be enforced on foreign banks in the same way, which is very unfair. Moreover, financial institutions registered abroad will inevitably increase in the future in order to escape the government's laws and regulations.

Coal Port

Resolution of Labor Dispute at the Loading and Unloading Docks 139

According to the Central News Agency, since the Capital Ferry on the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway at Xiaguan Coal Wharf began operation last year, the loading and unloading work has gradually decreased. The dockworkers, fearing unemployment, petitioned various agencies for relief. The Railway Bureau, recognizing the urgency of the workers' request, sent personnel to Nanjing to work with local agencies to develop a relief plan. However, due to the complexity of the issues and the involvement of the dispute over the dismissal of dockworkers at Pukou, the case remained unresolved for over a year. On the third of last month, the Railway Bureau again sent personnel to Nanjing, instructing the loading and unloading contractors to first register workers. At the same time, they assessed work performance and conducted physical examinations to determine who would stay and who would leave. As a result, 211 workers were qualified to stay, while 294 were dismissed. An agreement was reached with the workers, and with the sympathy of various agencies, the Railway Bureau allocated 5,000 silver dollars as relief funds for the dismissed workers. Except for those impersonating others, 135 workers were eligible for relief funds, totaling 4,820 silver dollars. This money was distributed on the 23rd of last month under the supervision of representatives from various agencies, and each dismissed worker received their share. The case was thus concluded. Unexpectedly, on the 26th, a group of dismissed workers, incited by others, again formed a group to petition and submitted a petition to the Railway Bureau, claiming that the relief method was unfair. Upon receiving this news, the Railway Bureau urgently dispatched Director Xiao of the Traffic Department and Director Ma of the Police Department to Nanjing on the 6th of this month to investigate. They immediately summoned representatives of the petitioners for talks at the station. As the representatives had not arrived, the Ministry of Railways convened another meeting on the 7th. The representatives presented the following demands: (1) Those who did not register by July 10th should be allowed to register retroactively, and those dismissed workers who were still strong and capable should be re-examined for re-employment; (2) They opposed the contractors and foremen who were retained; (3) Foremen of each team should be elected by the workers in the future. At that time, the Railway Bureau accepted the first and third demands, and agreed to consider the second. The representatives were also informed that within two days, they should provide a list of workers requesting retroactive registration and re-examination to Director Xiao for review. On the 8th, the Railway Bureau convened the representatives of the petitioners, contractors, and retained foremen at Xiaguan Station to discuss the steps to resolve the case, and also invited Director Xu of the Military Police Headquarters to attend. It was agreed on the spot that the first step would be to issue service certificates to the retained workers starting at 11:00 AM on August 10th; the second step would be to conduct retroactive registration and examination; and the third step would be to elect foremen. All parties agreed. On the 9th, the petitioners came to the station again to report difficulties, abruptly overturning the previous agreement and attaching many additional demands. The Railway Bureau repeatedly persuaded them to comply. Although the representatives seemed to agree on the surface, they gathered again on the morning of the 10th and went to the Ministry of Railways to continue their petition. Seeing that the representatives had repeatedly gone back on their word and could not be reasoned with, the Railway Bureau separately requested the Nanjing City Party Headquarters, the Nanjing City Social Affairs Bureau, the Police Department, the Military Police Headquarters, and the Ministry of Railways to send representatives to the station to supervise the issuance of service certificates to the retained workers, and requested the Military Police Headquarters and the Police Department to send additional troops and police to maintain order. Representatives from various agencies, including Wang Huibai, Zhou Jichang, You Siguang, Lang Zulin, and Wang Rongcheng from the Police Department, Pan Suizhang and Xu Qijie from the Military Police Headquarters, Xiong Yuemu from the Social Affairs Bureau, Sui Guanglu from the City Party Headquarters, and Section Chief Yin and Section Chief Yang from the Ministry of Railways, respectively issued service certificates to the retained workers starting at 11:00 AM. By 5:00 PM, 192 people had received their service certificates. Finally, Director Xiao explained the process of the Railway Bureau's handling of the case and urged the workers to work with peace of mind. Representatives from various agencies unanimously elected Director Pan of the Military Police Headquarters to deliver a speech, which was quite moving. During the distribution of the workers' service certificates, although some women made noise outside the station, the situation remained peaceful thanks to the effective maintenance of order by the military and police.

Agricultural and Commercial Bank to Open the Day After Tomorrow 140

Yesterday, a meeting of all bank staff was held.

Chen Gongbo will personally come to Shanghai to officiate the opening ceremony.

The Agricultural and Commercial Bank, jointly established by the Ministry of Industry with official and commercial capital, is fully prepared and has decided to officially open at 9:00 AM the day after tomorrow (the 15th). The candidates for the four section chiefs of the General Administration have also been decided. All important staff of the bank held a meeting yesterday to discuss various issues related to the opening. The banknotes previously stored in Beijing have also been transported to Shanghai in preparation for issuance. The news is recorded as follows:

Mr. Mei Returns to Shanghai, the General Manager of the Bank, Mr. Mei Zhezhi, went to Beijing on the 8th to meet with Minister Chen, inquire about the bank's operating policies, and report on the progress of preparations. After arriving in Beijing, he returned to Shanghai immediately because the opening date was approaching and there were many internal arrangements and tasks. He arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday. According to Mr. Mei, both the internal and external arrangements of the bank have been completed and it is scheduled to open on the 15th without further delay.

Four Section Chiefs The organization of the General Administration of the bank is divided into four sections: Document, Accounting, Business, and Issuance. Opening the Day After Tomorrow The bank issued a notice yesterday stating that the bank has raised a capital of 3 million yuan, which has been approved and registered by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, and has been approved to issue convertible banknotes. Simple Ceremony According to the secretary of the General Administration, there will be no special ceremony for the opening of the bank on the 15th, just like any ordinary bank. Banknotes Transported to Shanghai When the Agricultural Bank was established in 1923, it was approved by the government to issue banknotes. Therefore, after its restoration this time, it will issue the banknotes that were previously printed but not issued. The denominations are one yuan, five yuan, and ten yuan. The General Administration has sent personnel to Beijing to collect and transport the banknotes to Shanghai for issuance when the bank opens the day after tomorrow.

Tongshun and Ji'an Vessels

Collide on the Huangpu River at Lujiazui 145

The Ji'an's Upper Deck Damaged

The Tongshun Vessel Sails as Usual

The Datong Company's Tongshun vessel, which departed from Shanghai yesterday en route to the Yangtze River, collided with the Swire Company's Ji'an vessel, which was entering Shanghai, near the mouth of the Suzhou Creek at Lujiazui. The Ji'an's upper deck was damaged, while the Tongshun sailed as usual. The details are recorded below:

Collision The Tongshun vessel loaded cargo at the Ronglin Wharf in Nanshi at around 4:00 PM yesterday and set sail for Wuhu. At 5:30 PM, it collided with the Swire Company's Ji'an vessel, which was coming to Shanghai from the Yangtze River, near the Baidu Bridge outside the mouth of the Suzhou Creek at Lujiazui. At that time, it was low tide and the current was very rapid. The two vessels met and were already very close, so they could not avoid each other. The port and starboard sides of the two vessels collided. The Tongshun was a cargo ship without passengers, while the Ji'an had many passengers. The passengers were greatly alarmed during the collision, but fortunately there were no accidents.

Damage Although the two vessels collided, they were able to avoid each other effectively. Therefore, only the three upper decks on the starboard side of the Ji'an vessel were destroyed. The Tongshun vessel was not damaged. After the collision, both vessels stopped and hoisted flags to report to the Customs.

Inspection The River and Sea Customs Shipping Office saw the two vessels hoisting flags to report and immediately sent personnel to the scene to investigate. The water police also sent detectives to the scene to investigate. After the Customs officer inspected the damaged area of the Ji'an and inquired about the situation, the captains of both vessels signed their names for future negotiation. The Ji'an then sailed to the Yangjiadu Wharf in Pudong to dock, pending a report to the company today. The Tongshun vessel was not damaged and sailed as usual.

Negotiation Yesterday was Sunday and the Swire Company was closed as usual. There was no statement on the Ji'an's collision damage. The negotiation will take place after the captain's report today. On the Datong Company's side, a reporter went to the company to inquire at around 8:00 PM last night. According to an employee, Mr. Zhang, he only knew that the Tongshun vessel had departed and had not heard anything about the accident. The captain had not reported it either.

French Concession City Federation Branch

Continued News on Opposition to Water and Electricity Price Hikes 146

Emergency Meeting of the Fifth Branch of the City Federation

Notice to Members from the Fourth Branch

The stores and citizens of the French Concession in Shanghai are opposing the French water and electricity company's increase in deposit fees and disguised price hikes. The Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation Fifth Branch held an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss countermeasures. The Fourth District Branch issued a notice to its members, as follows:

Emergency Meeting of the Fifth Branch 147

The Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation Fifth District Branch held an emergency meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon to discuss countermeasures. More than ten committee members, including Yan Chengxian, Shang Mujiang, Wu Yunzhu, Zhang Qingfa, Hu Zifang, Qu Zhenhua, Xu Zixian, Zhang Huichang, Yuan Bingyuan, Fang Boqin, Cheng Zhusun, and Qian Liqun, attended the meeting. Chairman Gong Jingyan reported that the association had received a joint letter from the shops on Caishi Road, including Zhonghua Factory, Shuxintang, Ruichang, Lu Dachang, Yushun, Meiman, Xiangli, and Dashengshen, stating that the sudden increase in deposit fees by the French water and electricity company was unbearable in the current economic downturn, and requested negotiations on how to handle the case. After the committee members expressed their opinions, three resolutions were passed: (1) Send a letter to the French Municipal Council requesting the cancellation of the company's change of regulations and continue to operate according to the old regulations, so as to reduce the burden on the citizens; (2) Send a letter to the general association requesting the Municipal Council to negotiate on the basis of reason and strive to achieve the purpose of canceling the disguised price increase; (3) In addition to sending a letter to the Ratepayers' Association for negotiation, question the two Chinese directors, Lu Bohong and Zhu Yan, who participated in the Municipal Council, whether they expressed any objections when the company requested to increase the deposit fees, and ask whether Mr. Lu and Mr. Zhu have any mature rescue measures to comply with public opinion. Next, the meeting discussed the joint letter from the stores in Tangjiawan Market, including Xie Lixiang, requesting the ban on public toilets in the market in order to emphasize hygiene. It was resolved to forward it to the Municipal Government for prohibition. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Notice from the Fourth Branch 148

The Fourth District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation issued a special notice to its members yesterday stating: "Regarding the matter of notice, the French water and electricity company, in this time of economic recession and extreme economic decline, has suddenly increased the deposit fees, disregarding the suffering of the citizens, and arbitrarily increased prices in disguise. The association has repeatedly received requests from members to oppose it on the basis of reason and find ways to prevent the company from changing its regulations, so as to avoid disguised price increases and reduce the burden on the citizens. After an emergency meeting, it was resolved that in addition to sending a letter to the general association for negotiation and sending letters to the Chinese directors of the French Concession Ratepayers' Association to make suggestions to the French Municipal Council to stop the company from changing its regulations and strive to achieve the cancellation of the increase in deposit fees, all members should pay attention to all the company's actions. If any suspicious documents are found, please report to the association immediately so that negotiations can be based on them. The resolution has been recorded, and a special notice is hereby issued to all members to pay attention to it."

County Government

Instructs Township and Town Chiefs to Promote Subsidiary Occupations 149

The Shanghai County Government, in view of the fact that the production of flowers and rice are the main industries in the county, and that the people's livelihood is frequently endangered in times of famine, and that the promotion of subsidiary occupations, such as fish farming, bamboo planting, chicken raising, and planting flowers, fruits, and vegetables, costs little and yields great benefits, which is related to the development of the rural economy, specially instructed the newly appointed township and town chiefs in each district to carefully assess the local conditions and vigorously promote subsidiary occupations for farmers in the future, and to often lead farmers to visit the Qiangshu Horticultural School, which has achieved success in the county, in order to learn from it and benefit the people's livelihood.

More than 100 Tobacco and Exchange Businesses

Appeal to Maintain the Original Quota of Licenses 151

The Shanghai Tobacco and Exchange Business Association previously received a report from its member, Ding Ruitai, of Lao Baidu Street in Nanshi, stating that the tax for a Class D license for donated tobacco was 2 yuan per quarter, but now the investigators from the Shinan Tax Collection Office of the Finance Bureau said that it must be 20 yuan. It was also reported by Ding He Xiang, a member of Caojiadu Wujiaochang, that the tax for a Class D license for donated tobacco was 4 yuan per quarter, but now the investigators from the Shixi Tax Collection Office ordered them to obtain a 40-yuan license. In addition, they would have to donate 4 yuan, 8 yuan, or 12 yuan for each sale, which was undecided and requested a meeting to discuss. The members of the association were panicked upon hearing this news. Those who had registered did not dare to apply for the new licenses. Those who donated 2 yuan are now required to increase it to 4 yuan. More than 100 businesses, such as Damin Store on Anlan Road, jointly signed a letter to the association yesterday, sending all the license receipts to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting them to forward it to the Finance Bureau and maintain the original practice to show consideration and reduce the burden. The original letter is excerpted as follows: "Our stores, with a limited and extremely small scope, have been struggling to maintain their business and are barely able to pay taxes. In view of the commercial difficulties, the authorities have always listed our stores in the Class D tax bracket. Unexpectedly, in order to increase tax revenue, the Finance Bureau has disregarded the suffering of our industry and changed the Class D licenses of our stores to Class C, and Class C to Class B, implementing a double tax collection. Our stores are now experiencing sluggish business and have reached the extreme of suffering. Moreover, the competition among our neighbors is fierce, and it is not easy to make a small profit. How can we bear this heavy burden? The above situation is very clear. We hereby send this letter to your association, attaching the license receipts, and request you to forward it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and present the detailed situation to the Finance Bureau, explaining the plight of small businesses and the current economic downturn, and that our donations and taxes should be allowed to be paid according to the original quota. Not only will our stores benefit greatly, but all the businesses will be grateful. Please make efforts for our stores, and the Finance Bureau will definitely consider the commercial difficulties. " It is said that the association attaches great importance to this issue and has decided to call a joint meeting of the relevant tobacco and alcohol associations to make a final request to the authorities.

Second Special Court

Tomorrow's Burning of Opium and Toxic Substances 153

The Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Local Court stipulates that opium, morphine, drug pills, smoking paraphernalia, and gambling paraphernalia confiscated by the police shall be publicly burned every three months. There have been ten previous burnings on record. The opium and toxic substances and gambling paraphernalia confiscated during the three months from April to the end of June of this year are now scheduled to be publicly burned for the eleventh time at 2:00 PM tomorrow (the 14th) on the open space east of the court by President Wang Simo and Chief Prosecutor Chen Beisan. The High Court and the Ministry of Judicial Administration have been notified in advance, and the court has invited representatives from military, political, police, business, judicial, lawyer associations, and drug control associations in Shanghai to attend the event for supervision.

Shangde Lane

Seeking Court Relief for Rent Reduction Requests 154

The Shangde Lane Branch of the Third District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation has submitted a letter to the Third District Branch to forward it to the court for relief regarding the rent reduction movement. The original letter is recorded as follows: "To whom it may concern: We have recently received a letter from the Shangde Lane Branch stating that when the citizens rented houses in Shangde Lane, each family paid a small rent of 300 to 400 yuan. Recently, due to the economic downturn and the sluggish market, the rent reduction movement is an urgent need of the times, and it is also justified to demand the return of the illegally paid small rent. The landlord should accept this reasonable request as much as possible to maintain the relationship between the landlord and tenant. Not only will the citizens benefit and Shanghai prosper, but it will also be in this move. However, the landlord did not intend to do this, but used high-pressure tactics, using the excuse of rent arrears, and entrusted lawyer Qian Baohe to send a letter to Zhang Hongshan, Wang Damao, and others to recover the rent. The rent in Shangde Lane is more expensive than in other areas, and it is necessary to reduce the rent. And the small rent of 300 to 400 yuan paid when entering the house can be used to offset the rent, so the rent arrears are no longer a fact. We should ask your association to send a letter to the court to declare it, so as to avoid the landlord's obscuring the facts in court, causing losses that can be feared. The rent reduction movement is caused by the economic downturn, and the illegal small rent is strictly prohibited by law. The association's request for rent reduction and recovery of small rent are justified and are completely different from ordinary rent arrears. We hereby send this letter to your court, respectfully requesting your court to approve the record and provide relief according to law, so as to benefit the people. The president of the Second Special District Local Court, Sheng Zhiren, Standing Committee Member."

Hongqiao Sanatorium's Medical Report

Hongqiao Sanatorium Medical Report 155

The Shanghai West Hongqiao Sanatorium's medical report for last month is as follows: The sanatorium has a total of 50 beds and admitted 68 patients, including 39 cases of chronic bronchitis and neurasthenia. In addition, there were also several cases of people seeking summer relief and smoking cessation. There were 24 people who stayed for more than four weeks, of which 16 cases had a significant increase in weight. One Western woman even gained 16 pounds in weight in one month. The operating room performed a total of 6 major surgeries and 5 minor surgeries, mostly for nearby residents who had suffered accidental injuries. The X-ray department took a total of 26 X-rays, including 22 lung X-rays. The results showed that only 4 people had no lung disease, which shows the wide spread of lung disease in the city. The laboratory report showed that a total of 97 tests were performed last month. Local doctors, such as Gu Yuqi, Huang Zhong, Boli, Shen Chengwu, Yu Yunxiu, Cao Chentao, Shen Shubao, Zhuang De, Zang Boyong, Fei Zibin, Wang Yijing, Fang Jiacheng, Jin Wenqi, Engel, Feinerxiao, Chen Hongkang, Li Fen, and Luo Aisi, have all sent patients to the sanatorium for treatment and expressed their satisfaction with all the facilities and services of the sanatorium.

The Landlord Wins

The Lease is Terminated

The New World lawsuit, which has attracted the attention of Shanghai people, was caused by the landlord, Cheng Linsheng, suing the tenant, Qiu Peilin, for breach of contract, requesting termination of the lease (the location is the area around the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Xizang Road, i.e., the northern part of the New World and Fuyuan Lane). Discovery of a Sunken Ship off the Northern Coast 158

Hydrographic Office Notice to the Shipping Community

A sunken vessel has recently been discovered off the northern coast of the Bohai Bay, south of the Caofeidian shoals, 6.4 nautical miles at 186 degrees true north from the Caofeidian light buoy, approximately at 118 degrees 30 minutes east longitude and 38 degrees 50 minutes north latitude. As this location is a vital waterway, the Hydrographic Office, deeply concerned that passing ships might collide with it, hereby issues a notice to alert the shipping community to exercise caution.

Large Quantity of Narcotics Intercepted on the Shanghai-Minhang Road 159

At approximately 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, Chen Agou, a native of Xinzhuang who operates a shoe store and is a peddler of local products, was transporting narcotics from Shanghai. He was traveling on a long-distance bus on the Shanghai-Minhang road to the town of Zhuanqiao, when he was spotted by a police officer stationed there. Robbery Conviction at the Yesheng Pawnshop 160

Shen Wancai Sentenced to Seven Years in Prison

On June 12th, at approximately 3:00 AM, four robbers broke into the Yesheng Pawnshop at 1246 Huade Road, brandishing guns to silence any resistance. They stole jewelry and silver dollars worth over 200 yuan and fled. On the morning of the 4th of this month, at 4:30 AM, detectives Xia Shouqi and Hou Fulin of the Yangshupu Police Station apprehended Shen Wancai, a native of Funing and a member of the robbery gang, in a straw hut on Mayushan Road in Zhabei. They found two rows of bullets on his person, totaling 19, 30 yuan in paper currency, a handgun, six bullets, two knives, and a bag of stolen silver jewelry on his bed. He was taken to the First Special District Court, where he claimed that the guns, bullets, and jewelry were stored there by Han Er, who was at large, and that he did not participate in the robbery. However, Yang Hai, a shop employee, testified that he saw him at the scene holding a handgun. He was detained for further investigation. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan presided over the continued hearing in the Third Criminal Court. Mr. Ru Baoyi, the lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that the defendant had fully confessed to the crime at the police station and presented the confession for review, requesting a severe sentence. The defendant confessed that he was invited by Han Er, who was at large, to participate in the robbery. He said that Zhang San, Chen Jinbiao, and two others were also involved, and that he received 66 yuan after the robbery. Judge Wu sentenced Shen Wancai to seven years in prison. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the sentence, with two days of detention counting as one day of imprisonment. The guns, bullets, and knives were confiscated, and the stolen goods were returned.

Recent News from the South District Rent Reduction Committee 163

The South Shanghai District Rent Reduction Committee of Shanghai received a joint petition from the tenants of Qingyu Lane on Xietu Road, requesting the committee to seek a rent reduction from the landlord. The committee sent a letter to the landlord, Liu Qingyu, who repeatedly stated that the rent was already low and presented evidence from the March 1st edition of the Xinwen Bao newspaper that a rent reduction had already been granted. The committee, adhering to its principles, will commend landlords who have already reduced rent to acknowledge their benevolence. However, the committee believes the tenant's desire to reduce rent again is unreasonable and has strictly forbidden it. Recently, Mr. Wang Yueling, the landlord of Tongda Company on Minguo Road, personally visited the committee to discuss a rent reduction, agreeing to the following contract: Rent Reduction Mediation Agreement (Mediation Address): South Shanghai District Rent Reduction Committee. (Rent Calculation): Previous rent was 260 yuan, now 221 yuan. (Mediation Result): 85% discount, totaling 221 yuan. (Rent Reduction Period): From May 1934 to December 1937. After one year, both parties should act in good faith and make adjustments based on market conditions, but neither party should take extreme measures. (Mediator): South Shanghai District Rent Reduction Committee. (Tenant): Landlord Wang Yueling, Tenants Chen Shengtao and others. (Witness): Shen Xinfu, Standing Committee Member of the South District Rent Reduction Committee. Each party will retain a copy of the above mediation agreement for their records. Furthermore, after receiving the committee's letter advising a rent reduction, the landlord of Chengzhi Lane on Jingxiu Road not only failed to respond but also entrusted the management of the properties to the French accountant Daley & Co. After receiving a report from the tenants of Chengzhi Lane, the committee issued a notice: "To whom it may concern, We have recently received a report from Gu Xiayun, the representative of Chengzhi Lane, stating that the lane has submitted a request for rent reduction to your committee, resulting in a letter to the landlord Chengzhi Company. The landlord has repeatedly sent representatives to negotiate, only promising Xiayun personal rent reduction benefits, but not for the entire lane. We believe that rent reduction is a matter of maintaining the livelihood of the entire community. Xiayun is a resident of the same lane and also a petitioner for rent reduction. Why should she seek illegal personal benefits in the name of the group? Therefore, we politely refused and instructed the representative to negotiate directly with the South District Rent Reduction Committee. The representative, realizing her scheme had failed, suddenly posted a blatant announcement by Daley & Co., a French accountant, in the lane on the 4th of this month, stating that Daley & Co. would manage the properties from August 1st onwards. Moreover, the Chengzhi Company did not formally notify us beforehand. This action clearly abandons China's inherent civilization and disregards the obligation to help each other in times of crisis, using foreign influence to undermine the prosperity of the South District. Apart from declaring our disapproval, we will not accept any intervention by foreigners in the interaction between Chinese people until the issue of mutual assistance between Chinese and humans is resolved. We implore for assistance to uphold the livelihood of the people." The committee notes that it sent a letter to the landlord Chengzhi Company on May 16th regarding the request for rent reduction from the lane, along with No. 2 Tianzhutang Street and No. 2 South Gaoshou Lane on Zhabei Haining Road. The landlord disregarded the committee's earnest appeals and incited Gu Xiayun and others to sow discord by employing unclear foreign tactics, undermining the peaceful residence of the citizens of the South District, which is truly heartbreaking. The committee believes that the rent reduction movement is a necessary awakening for both landlords and tenants. For example, after receiving the committee's letter urging a rent reduction, the landlord Ding of the Kuangda Tea Company on Minguo Road immediately agreed to a rent reduction and abolished the original management to compensate for the loss during the rent reduction period. The committee deeply admires landlords who understand the greater good. However, the committee hopes that landlords will not stop employing doormen or property managers due to rent reduction, so as not to cause more unemployment in society. Now, during the citywide rent reduction mobilization, the landlord Wu of Chengzhi Lane not only does not seek to benefit his compatriots but actually invests in entrusting a foreign merchant, revealing his intentions through his actions. For the sake of peace, the committee sincerely hopes that the landlord, with the compassion of a Chinese, will join hands to revive the ailing Shanghai market, fulfilling the obligation of helping each other in times of crisis to resolve the rent reduction issue. The committee also hopes that Daley & Co., with the spirit of friendship between our nations, will not join in during this period of Sino-foreign cooperation for revival and put themselves in a difficult position before the rent reduction issue is resolved. On the tenant side, it is necessary to act in accordance with the committee's regulations and not default on rent under the pretext of rent reduction, otherwise, landlords will use this as an excuse, leading to unrest instead of peace. We hope that both parties will make concessions to avoid causing disputes. In addition to informing all parties, we hereby issue this public notice.

Because of the high rent and the owners not following the Municipal Government's regulations regarding original rent amounts, the West City Chen Yingshi Jianjiao Tsui Tanan Ba Business Shops are requesting reductions but the owners have ignored the request, causing disputes. Repercussions from the Demolition of Houses in Leyi Lane, French Concession 165

The houses in Leyi Lane on Nanyangqiao Annakin Road in the French Concession, totaling over thirty buildings, are the property of the Chinese businessman Jiang Hanzhai and are managed by the Teepack Property Department. The houses are relatively new and quite sturdy. Recently, the owner suddenly instructed the management office to notify the tenants that the houses are dilapidated and should be rebuilt immediately, ordering all tenants to move out by the end of August of this year, with water cut off and barricades erected on July 25th. All the tenants were immediately alarmed. Everyone believed that the owner had previously announced demolition, and representatives were sent to request a postponement, which was granted, with a letter from the management office as proof. This reversal of words is suspicious, and the houses are in good condition. Forced demolition and eviction of tenants under the current economic downturn are inappropriate. A unanimous objection was raised, and a report was filed with the Fourth District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District City Federation. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, a general meeting was held at the federation's headquarters to discuss countermeasures. Over thirty tenants attended, along with Director Dong Wenli, Ye Ruizhai, Committee Member Tong Lizhang, and Xu Yanwu from the Fourth District City Federation Branch, who attended to provide guidance. Li Yuting was publicly elected as chairman. After the report, the following countermeasures were resolved: (1) All tenants firmly expressed their opposition, vowing not to move out under any pressure. (2) The good condition of the lane and the owner's oppressive actions will be reported to the Party and government authorities and various organizations, advocating for fairness and preventing the demolition. (3) A letter will be sent to the Fourth Branch of the Civic Association in this district to fully negotiate and ensure the revocation of the demolition order. (4) Unite and establish an alliance agreement, refraining from any disruptive actions to facilitate negotiations. (5) Investigate details of rent arrears and deposit all rents into a bank for safekeeping. (6) Li Yuting, Wang Dekui, and Tang Baoshan were designated as tenant representatives. (7) If necessary, retain a lawyer as a legal advisor to safeguard our rights and interests. The meeting adjourned.

City News 172

After the end of 1933, if an increase or decrease was desired, the agreement of both parties was required. Unexpectedly, in the spring of 1933, the Gao Yi real estate agency took over the management of the lane and suddenly wanted to overturn the previous agreement and increase the rent. Reading Q&A

On the Philosophy of Life 199

Why do people come into the world? Is it for enjoyment? To transform society? Or for other reasons? Many readers have written to ask about this question. The readers who raise this question all feel that they don't know what attitude to take towards life. In other words, they cannot determine their own philosophy of life.

Speaking about life in a vague and general way will never yield any results. A person suddenly comes into the world for a trip, and then suddenly dies after a few decades. If they encounter illness or disaster along the way, they may lose their life before even reaching those decades. In their own life, they sometimes commit sins and sometimes accomplish great things, but they all come naked and return empty-handed. If you ask what it's all for, it's really impossible to say for sure. Since we can't say why, doesn't that mean that life is not worth the slightest bit of attachment? Yet the reality is not like that. Everyone is attached to their own life, and everyone hopes to prolong their own life. What do they want to do by prolonging it? Again, no one can give a reason.

Therefore, hedonistic poets like Li Bai and Su Shi say: "Life is nothing more than a dream, meaningless. Let's enjoy ourselves and indulge in the intoxication of dreams!" But if they believe that life is a dream, a deceiving illusion, then why be attached to the intoxication of dreams? Why not just commit suicide and avoid a meaningless existence of being drunk in life and dreaming of death? This is the contradiction of hedonists, and they cannot answer it themselves.

Philosophers of idealism say that life is meaningful, and people should adhere to a supreme moral ideal to live their lives, strive for this ideal, and sacrifice for it. Life is not important; what is important is the moral ideal. But if we pursue the matter to the end and ask: Yes, assuming that life is for this moral ideal, why must we come for the sake of the ideal? Everyone is born the same way and dies the same way. People with ideals do not necessarily live a few decades longer, and people without ideals do not necessarily fail to survive. Why must there be ideals? Why is it not okay to have no ideals? This is also an unanswerable contradiction.

Therefore, talking about life in a vague and general way will not lead to any results. We must find the meaning of life in concrete facts.

In fact, the first important condition for a person in the world is the society in which they are born. Everyone is born in a specific society; no one lives in the sky. Society precedes the individual, so the individual's life and actions are all determined by the social situation. People in feudal societies have the characteristics of feudal life, and people in capitalist societies also have their own special lives. And in these two societies, people are divided into different classes due to differences in status and property, and each class has its own life.

Each society and each class has its own special life, and these various special lives form various special thoughts. For example, nobles and monarchs in feudal societies have a particularly superior right, and their lives are built on this superior right. Therefore, they hope that people respect their privilege, which gives rise to the ideas of privilege and loyalty to the monarch. In their view, the duty of loyalty to the monarch is more important than life itself. The idea of loyalty is a typical philosophy of life in the feudal order. For example, in capitalist society, the lives of capitalists are based on capital and property relations, so they attach particular importance to capital and wealth. They believe that capital and property are more important than feudal privileges. Therefore, during the French Revolution, they raised the banner of freedom and equality to oppose the privilege system. Their lives made them develop the ideas of freedom and equality (of course, their freedom and equality could only be enjoyed with property and capital, so this freedom and equality was a false freedom and equality). Freedom and equality became their philosophy of life. (But this only refers to the capitalists of the first half of the nineteenth century.)

In this way, we can know that a person's philosophy of life is determined by their social environment. The aforementioned semi-pessimistic and semi-hedonistic philosophy of life of Li Bai and Su Shi represents the lives of those frustrated scholar-officials in the feudal era. If you ask vaguely what life is for, you will get nothing in the end. But if we focus on society, we can know that when a person is born into the world, their purpose is the purpose stipulated by the society in which they live. The answer to why life exists lies here.

However, society is made up of everyone. Everything in society is the sum of human behavior. Although individual behavior is essentially determined by the conditions of the whole society, people are not completely passive. Within a certain range, there can still be relative freedom. Although our philosophy of life is largely a product of society, there are various classes and various lives in a certain society, and there is not only one kind of philosophy of life. There is room for us to choose. We must choose the most correct philosophy of life as our compass for life.

The method of selection was debated by many scholars in China's "Debate on Science and Philosophy of Life" ten years ago. Among them, one faction advocated choosing with free will, arguing that there is no fixed standard for the philosophy of life. We certainly do not agree with this. We believe that we must find a standard to determine the most correct world view.

To have a correct philosophy of life, we must first have a correct understanding of society. To have a correct understanding of society, we must study social sciences. In this sense, we can say that the philosophy of life should be determined by science.

As for asking: Is life for enjoyment? Is it to transform society? This question is not very important. As long as we have a correct knowledge of social science, then these questions will naturally be easily solved.

Qiu Feihai Defeats Ota 202

Wins Two Sets Consecutively, 6-4, 6-2

Ota Meets His Match, Utterly Helpless

Today Old Qiu Will Play Ota Again at Kangti Road

Ota, a former representative from the All-Japan Taikai Cup, etc., gave his second performance in Shanghai yesterday. Ota, who had defeated Lin Baohua the day before, played against Qiu Feihai yesterday. Qiu unexpectedly defeated Ota two sets to zero, winning easily 6-4, 6-2. The applause from the audience shook the sky. Qiu Feihai's performance yesterday reached its peak, with many wonderful moments, causing Ota to fall into a state of utter helplessness. In the doubles match, Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia defeated Kotera Yoshizo 6-3, 6-3, also very easily. In another singles match, Carlson defeated Kotera two sets to one, 2-6, 6-3, 6-3. Today, Ota and others will perform at the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club on Kangti Road, where Ota will play Qiu Feihai again. On Wednesday, they will perform at the Chinese Lawn Tennis Club. Yesterday's match report is as follows:

Lin and Zheng Win in Doubles 203

In the doubles match, Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia played against Kotera and Yoshida. Watanabe, who was originally scheduled to participate, was absent due to other commitments. Lin and Zheng won two sets consecutively, 6-3, 6-3, in an instant. Kotera was passable, but Yoshida was weak and incompetent, with many mistakes. Their skills were far apart. Lin served first, and the opponent won. Kotera served, and Lin and Zheng won four games in a row, taking the lead 4-1 effortlessly. In the fifth game, Lin served and won with a slip game, resulting in 5-2 and then 6-3, with Lin and Zheng winning the first set. In the second set, Kotera served first, and the server won each game, until the seventh game after 3-3, when Yoshida's serve was broken. Lin and Zheng then won four games in a row, 6-3, winning the second set again.

Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia (6-3, 6-3) Kotera and Yoshida

Qiu Feihai Overcomes Ota 204

Same Stroke Style: Qiu Feihai and Ota have completely identical stroke styles, with long baseline rallies going back and forth, sweeping diagonally across the court. Qiu Feihai occasionally went to the net a few times. Ota also switched to going to the net after failing in a rally yesterday, but it was ineffective. Therefore, the two were like a pair of sticky candies, causing laughter throughout the court.

Old Qiu's Masterpiece: Yesterday's match was entirely a confrontation of long baseline rallies. Whoever could maintain their composure and avoid panic would gain the final victory. This battle was nothing short of a triumphant masterpiece for Qiu Feihai in his life. His shots were stable, rarely going out of bounds. His diagonal shots landed deep in the corner, causing Ota to struggle. Ota's only weapon, his powerful forehand, was also ineffective yesterday. Qiu was able to respond to his various shots, while Ota became even more chaotic afterward, leading to a complete collapse.

Two 5-0s: Yesterday, the two ships almost had the same situation. Qiu Feihai led 5-0 in the first set, and the second set was also in the same situation, 5-0. Old Qiu's momentum was surprisingly strong, and both sets had the potential to be 6-0. Qiu Feihai served first, with baseline rallies going back and forth, one shot going back and forth about a dozen or twenty times. The first game ended after four deuces, with Qiu winning. Ota started to show his panic after failing in the intense first game. Qiu took advantage of the momentum and won five games in a row. Although Ota was angry in the fourth game and swung his powerful forehand, it had no effect. After 5-0, Ota made a desperate effort. Qiu had the lead 40-15 twice, but Ota won, making it 5-4. Ota served in the tenth game but failed to maintain it, and Qiu won 6-4.

Ota Succumbs: Starting from the second set, Ota was exhausted, and his shots lacked confidence. Even the easiest shots were sent into the net. He declined rapidly and was beyond salvation. Old Qiu repeatedly won five games in a row, putting Ota in a desperate situation. Although Ota tried his best to win back two games, Qiu Feihai won the final game with a slip game, winning the second set again 6-2.

Qiu Feihai (6-4, 6-2) Ota

Carlson Defeats Kotera 205

The last singles match, Carlson vs. Kotera, was no longer as tense and exciting. Kotera is a junior champion in Japan, young and skilled. His shots are stable, and the diagonal shots and the landing points of the ball are unpredictable. He won the first set 6-2 against Carlson, but he gradually showed panic afterward. Carlson won the next two sets 6-3, 6-3.

Carlson (2-6, 6-3, 6-3) Kotera

Hebei Wins Men's Team Championship 210

Qingdao Sweeps All Women's Events to Win Championship

Women's 100-Meter Freestyle Breaks North China Record

(Central News Agency, Peiping, 12th) The 12th was the second day of the North China Swimming Competition. The finals began at 8:30 AM. The number of spectators decreased slightly. A refreshing autumn breeze blew in the morning, and athletes from various regions engaged in the final battle in the rippling blue waves. The atmosphere was quite tense. Although Qingdao had hopes for the championship, their swimming skills were insufficient, and the sea monster Yan Renying did not participate. Their strength was lacking. However, Dong Jingchun was calm and experienced, and gained unexpected results. In the finals of various events, except for He Wenya's 100-meter freestyle, which broke the North China record, there were no other special achievements. As a result, Hebei won the first place in the men's team total score. Qingdao only won the first place in the women's team total score. Shandong suffered a disastrous defeat and returned. Only Zhou Changying from the four units of the Northeast worked hard, but it was to no avail. The entire competition was completed at 12:00 noon. The closing ceremony was held. The chairman, Yuan Liang, delegated the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Cai Yuan, to represent him due to other commitments. The ceremony was performed as scheduled. Afterwards, Cai gave a speech, expressing his deep apologies for the inadequate facilities. After the speech, he invited Mrs. He Yingqin, Wang Wenxiang, to present the awards. The closing ceremony ended successfully at 1:30 PM. At 4:00 PM, Yuan Liang hosted a banquet for all athletes and officials of the competition at the Municipal Government. Qingdao athletes planned to visit various scenic spots starting on the 13th and take the train south on the evening of the 14th. Hebei athletes would return to Tianjin in triumph on the 13th. Shandong would also return to Jinan on the same train.

(Peiping, 12th) The North China Swimming Competition continued at the swimming pool from 8:30 AM on the morning of the 12th. There were nearly 1,000 spectators, slightly less than on the 11th. Athletes from various units took the field on time. However, many representatives from Shandong Province did not arrive, with only two participating. By 12:00 noon, all events had been completed. Only Qingdao female athlete He Wenya broke the North China record in the 100-foot freestyle with a time of one minute and ten seconds. After the competition, the closing ceremony was held, and Mrs. He Yingqin, Wang Wenxiang, personally presented the awards. At 4:00 PM, Yuan Liang hosted a tea party at the Municipal Government to entertain the athletes and staff from various provinces and cities. On the evening of the 12th, Hebei athletes returned to Tianjin, and Shandong athletes returned to Jinan on the 13th. Qingdao athletes took a short tour and returned to Qingdao on the 14th. In the overall results, Hebei dominated the men's division, and Qingdao naturally won the championship in the women's division due to the absence of competitors.

(Peiping, 12th) Team Total Score: (1) Hebei 56 points, (2) Qingdao 51 points, (3) Jin 22 points, (4) Ping 9 points, (5) Lu 1 point. In the women's division, only Qingdao participated, 45 points.
